### Test One
* Sell when the price hits the upper line of the 20p 1std bollinger
* No Stoploss
* Results:
```
Total Trades: 70
Percent Up: 28.57
Percent Down: 71.43
Total Points Moved Down: 63.25
Potential Profit: 31625.00
Total Points Ups: 153.00 Count Ups: 20
Total Points Downs: 216.25 Count Downs: 50

## STOPLOSS OF 10

### Test Fifty-Six
* Sell when price hits the middle line of the 20p bollinger
* Stoploss is -10 points
* Results:
```
Total Trades: 70
Percent Up: 30.00
Percent Down: 70.00
Total Points Moved Down: -11.25
